See the GNU General Public License\nfor more details.\n\nYou should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License\nalong with GCC; see the file COPYING3.  If not see\n<http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.  */\n\n/* Basic block counter.\n\n   This is a simple GIMPLE optimization pass that counts the number of\n   basic blocks in each function and outputs the result to the dump file.\n\n   This pass demonstrates the standard GCC pattern for writing a\n   GIMPLE optimization pass:\n   1. Define a pass_data struct with metadata\n   2. Inherit from gimple_opt_pass\n   3. Implement gate() and execute() virtual methods\n   4.
